Suzhou 74

Wujiang Water Patrol Team Opens Fire to Suppress Bandits. Tan Guobin, captain of the Wujiang County Water Patrol Team, led four ships on the 13th of this month and set off to patrol the Zhenze area. On the 18th night, they encountered dozens of bandits on three ships in Ye Port, Taihu Lake. They opened fire and suppressed them, resulting in a fierce battle for half an hour. As a result, they rescued a hostage named Ni Fubao and seized a bandit ship and two rifles. Yesterday (21st), they brought them back to Wujiang and handed them over to the county for investigation.

Liyang Knife Bandit Fake Chief of Staff Surrenders and is Detained. Cai Hanyu (Lao Wu), the leader of the Liyang Knife Bandit, was arrested and executed in Shanghai. Ge Jinghe, the fake chief of staff under Cai, suddenly came to Suzhou on the 21st to surrender to the Higher Procuratorate. Chief Prosecutor Wang opened a court hearing to investigate. According to the confession, he was 31 years old and lived in Qinghe Bridge, three miles outside the West Gate of Liyang. After the case occurred, he was detained by the county government and released by his uncle Ge Leshan and his brother Ge Zihua. He is currently working in the Jinpu Road Machinery Office in Jinan, Shandong, introduced by his cousin who is an engineer on the road. Because the arrest warrant arrived in Jinan, he came to Suzhou to surrender. He also said that the chief of staff when Cai occupied the city was actually Ge Rongjing, a former member of the Party Department, not himself. As a result of the High Court's investigation, the circumstances were serious. He will be detained and the original guarantors, Ge Leshan, will be summoned for further investigation before being submitted to the court for verification.

Jiangdu Prison Case Appeal Pronounced. In the Jiangdu County court collapse case, the former head of the detention center, Liu Baichuan, and others were sentenced to five years of imprisonment. After the appeal to the Suzhou High Court, the two guards Wang Jiren and Chen Shulin were sentenced to five years of imprisonment. One guard, Lu Damaozi, was sentenced to two years. The former head of the detention center, Liu Baichuan, and the guards Wei Benli, Cheng Liuxing, Zhou Wenbiao, Chen Guixing, and Tu Guilin were each sentenced to eight months.

Ancient Tomb in Nan Yuan is Robbed. The Wuzhong Tomb Protection Association reported to Yizhi that four coffins of lacquered Nanmu wood were found excavated in the Caodian side behind the Xinsu Farm on Nan Yuan Shang in Fengmen. More than thirty pieces of tomb boundary stone in the excavated area were all excavated. Only one piece remains. It is said that this Nanmu coffin has been around for many years, perhaps dating back to the Song Dynasty. It is difficult to determine because the main tomb has not been found. Moreover, the excavation is not only in this one place in Nan Yuan Shang, but also in the wasteland near the Public Sports Ground and Yanzi Temple. Hundreds of corpses have been excavated, and the bones are exposed, which is very tragic. After the association received the report, on the afternoon of the 20th, the committee members Zhang Zhongren and Li Yinquan, accompanied by County Chief Huang, brought a photographer from Liucun Photography Studio to inspect Nan Yuan Shang first. Unexpectedly, the four lacquered ancient Nanmu coffins had been stolen. According to the residents of the area, the excavators were all from Jiangbei, hired by people from Shanghai. The photographer was immediately ordered to photograph the excavated area and the police from the Second Branch were ordered to guard it and investigate the excavators and thieves. They then went to the back of the Public Sports Ground to investigate. It was learned that Wang Jintai and Pan Rixuan, who grew vegetables there, were suspected of being involved in the case. The First Branch summoned them to the bureau for questioning. According to their confession, they did not know about the private excavation of the cemetery. They were transferred by the bureau to the Public Security Bureau and then to the county for questioning and detention.

Bandit Ship Found in Xihua Township, Guangfu. At 3:00 pm on the 20th, five or six bandit ships with more than 100 bandits fully armed were found in Xihua Township, Guangfu. The police team stationed there telegraphed the city for assistance. Also, at 9:00 pm on the 20th, two bandit ships arrived at Zhaojiashang Village, four miles southeast of Chefang Township, and kidnapped residents Zhao Hongzhang and Zhao Yuzhu and took them to Cheng Lake.

Changshu 78

A Water Police officer negligently kills someone. Zhang, a barber in Yangshuyuan Town, Yuanhe District, has a son who is married to a woman surnamed Mou, who is in her thirties. On the afternoon of the 18th, Lin Desheng, a soldier from the Second Squad of the Thirteenth Detachment of the Water Police stationed there, went to Zhang's barbershop for a haircut. The soldier was wearing his uniform and a Mauser pistol on his belt. When he was getting a haircut, he took off the gun and belt. After the haircut, Lin put the gun back on his belt. Zhang then jokingly said, "What's this thing for?" Lin Desheng replied, "This is a Mauser pistol, it can kill people. Do you want to try it? I'll kill you." As he spoke and laughed, he held the Mauser pistol in his hand and pretended to aim, and pulled the trigger. Unexpectedly, the Mauser pistol was loaded with live ammunition and was not on safe, so the bullet fired when the trigger was pulled. Zhang was standing next to Lin, but luckily was not hit. However, his daughter-in-law was working behind him, and the bullet hit her lower abdomen on the left side, and she immediately fell to the ground unconscious. The whole family panicked and immediately grabbed Lin Desheng. At the same time, someone was sent to report to the district office, the Twelfth Sub-Bureau, and the Water Police Department. Inspector Guo Guoyu and Inspector Wang Yunying of the Public Security Sub-Bureau arrived at the scene one after another. The injured woman was taken to the Jishan Hospital in the city by water patrol boat for treatment. Meanwhile, the murderer Lin Desheng was taken back to the headquarters. However, the woman died due to excessive bleeding.

A meat ticket escapes danger in Fukou, Fushan. Lu, a farmer from Changxiang in Fukou Town, Fushan District, was kidnapped by bandits to Jiangbei at midnight on December 30th of last year. Those kidnapped at the same time included Lu's son, nephew, and a Miss Tang, a total of four people. Later, the bandits sent a letter demanding 50,000 yuan. Since Lu was not wealthy and could not raise such a huge sum, he entrusted someone to negotiate repeatedly. As a result, he was redeemed for 5,200 yuan and has now returned home across the river.

Zhenjiang 80

A sudden storm arises in the Jiang silk industry. Jiang silk was the most famous product of this port during the Qing Dynasty. After the revolution, it declined sharply and has not been able to recover to this day. However, there are still five to six thousand workers who depend on it for a living. They are divided into two types: those who work on “che” (carriage) machines, numbering about 4,000 workers in 200 households, and those who work on “ji” (loom) machines, numbering about 1,500 workers in 300 households. The "che" industry (meaning the warp industry) used to produce four colors during the Qingming season for flowers and fruits: antique bronze, golden yellow, and blackish-yellow. They would send 78 taels of goods (silk) to the loom industry to be woven into 100 taels of silk. Since the introduction of foreign dyes, the representatives of the dyeing industry and the warp industry agreed that 75 taels should be considered as 100 taels. Last year, the warp and loom industries each elected ten representatives to sign an agreement to be observed. Now, unscrupulous elements in the loom industry are causing trouble, and the already agreed agreement has been broken. They are now acting independently, causing disputes between the two industries from time to time. Until the other day, the warp industry stopped work en masse due to cost concerns, as a passive resistance. Although there were people mediating, neither side had a real representative, making it difficult to negotiate. However, the loom industry is linked to the warp industry. When the warp industry stops, the loom industry has no silk to weave, and will soon stop as well. Although those who are not currently stopped have stock to weave, they will soon stop as well. If this dispute continues, the livelihood of thousands of workers will be severely affected. It is hoped that the authorities will pay attention to this and quickly mediate to avoid any complications.

The Jiangsu Police School is temporarily difficult to relocate. Recently, the Jiangsu Provincial Police School, due to the fact that the Guard Division intends to be stationed in Zhenjiang, the Ministry of Military Affairs intends to take back the barracks used by the school. The school had surveyed an address in Nantong in preparation for relocation. It is now heard that the school originally intended to relocate to Nantong immediately, but due to the emptiness of the provincial treasury, repairs and relocation would cost at least 20,000 yuan. Furthermore, the school will hold its graduation ceremony within the next forty to fifty days. If the relocation is carried out, there would be many inconveniences, so the talk of relocation is difficult to realize for the time being.

Yangzhou 81

Local villagers at Tianmu Temple obstruct road construction. When construction started on the Jiangsu Provincial Highway Gua Yu Road Yang You Section, which belongs to sections one through five (place name Tianmu Temple) of Jiangdu’s Seventh District, on the 15th, hundreds of local villagers suddenly arrived to obstruct the road construction. They demanded that the fields, houses, and graves in the area not be touched, only then would they allow the road construction. The Director of the Yu Construction Bureau separately telegraphed the Pacification Superintendent’s Office, the Construction Department, and the County Government, requesting them to send teams for assistance. He also went to the province to meet Director Sun to ask for instructions. The department ordered the county to send a team to protect the construction and punish the ringleaders. On the previous day, Director Yu, together with the police team of the Public Security Bureau, led the team to Shao to supervise and urge the continuation of the work. However, as soon as they arrived at the construction site, hundreds of female villagers had gathered there, each holding farm tools and dirty objects, and continued to petition to obstruct the road construction. Although the Director and others tried their best to persuade them, they could not stop them. They were also aggressively trying to attack Director Yu. With the protection of the road guards, he was able to escape. Seeing that Yu had left, the villagers went to the Chamber of Commerce and the District Office to petition, with the same goal as before. Some of the villagers, due to hunger, took food from the cake shops at will. Seeing this situation, the shops went to the camp headquarters to report and requested that a team be sent to maintain order together with the road police. The villagers misunderstood the soldiers as the Bao An Tuan (security corps) and a conflict arose. The camp headquarters took ten female villagers away. Seeing that the military police were arresting people, some villagers rushed into the camp headquarters. Only after extreme restraint were they dispersed.

Gaoyou 82

Bandits rob and kill in Da Lu Township. The family of Lu Anqing, the head of Da Lu Township in the Sixth District of the county, was suddenly attacked by more than ten bandits armed with guns on the night before. After entering the door, they immediately opened fire and killed Lu. Lu's son was also shot and injured when he stepped forward to help. They then looted everything. Lu's wife, Jia, has gone to the county government to report the crime and request a strict investigation.

Pinghu 83

Water police kill a large number of bandits. Zhou Weilie, the director of the Second District of Zhejiang Inland Water Police, arrived in Pinghu on the 19th to supervise Wu Kun, the captain of the Ninth Team, and his troops, as well as the patrol team, to suppress bandits in the eastern township. They saw a bandit boat sailing in the sea off Baisha Bay. Zhou and others hired three sea boats to pursue them. They came into contact with the bandits on the Ling Hai sea area bordering Jiangsu and Zhejiang and fought fiercely for three hours. Thirty to forty bandits were killed on the spot. A bandit boat was captured, containing a hostage named Zhu from Fengxian County, Jiangsu, four rapid-firing guns, and ten wooden boxes of ammunition. They were immediately escorted back to the district headquarters.

Ningbo 84

A major fire in Jiangxia. The head of Jiangxia Street in Yu Bu is a bustling area with closely packed shops. Unexpectedly, at 7:30 PM last night (the 19th), the Damei Watch Shop on the three-story building caught fire for unknown reasons. The fire was very fierce and was not extinguished until 8:30 PM. After investigation, it was found that the following buildings were burned: one building of Damei Watch Shop, one building of Xinxintai Glass Shop, one building of Hengtai Bowl Shop, one building of Xixing Barber Shop, one building of Jintai Tobacco and Paper Shop, two buildings of Taihe Exchange Shop, two buildings of Fang Yihe Warehouse, and two buildings of Chunsheng Yang Candy Shop, with a total loss of fifty to sixty thousand yuan. Among them, Fang Yihe, Taihe, and Chunsheng Yang suffered the most.

A fishing boat from the Aquatic Products School causes trouble in Yong. Eighteen crew members of the Xinfuxing steamboat, which was berthed at Xiabaisha in the Yong River, sailed a sampan at about 7 PM yesterday (the 19th) planning to take a night cruise in the Jiangxin of Xiabaisha. Unexpectedly, when the sampan was just driven to the Jiangxin, it happened that the Minsheng No. 2 fishing boat of the Dinghai Aquatic Products School arrived in Yong. The two sides were unable to avoid each other, resulting in a collision. The middle of the sampan was broken and sank immediately. All 18 crew members fell into the river. Thirteen people were rescued. The other five people, including Zhulin, Yin Heshang, Jiang Busheng, Zhu Jincan, and Le Aquan, were drowned. After the accident, the Zhejiang Customs sent personnel to detain the Minsheng No. 2 fishing boat. The Xinfuxing steamboat also arrested the first mate of the fishing boat, Su Chengzhou, and detained him temporarily at the First Sub-Bureau of the Second District on the Jiangbei shore, awaiting resolution.

Education News Highlights

Ministry of Education orders students to wear uniforms. 85

Starting this summer, the Ministry of Education has ordered all schools at all levels to uniformly wear uniforms, notifying the education bureaus of all provinces and cities. The Training Directorate-General's letter states that the student uniforms were previously stipulated and circulated for implementation by your ministry. Recently, the military instructors of various schools have reported to this department that while many schools can earnestly comply with the regulations, some schools do not pay attention to this matter. The school feels that the spirit is not invigorated, and the military training also feels that there are many obstacles. It is proposed to transfer the consultation to strictly order the implementation of various schools to facilitate education. At present, it is necessary to rectify the school spirit and cultivate the habit of discipline, integrity and simplicity. Therefore, clothing should not be allowed to take all kinds of forms to express the spirit of distraction and the atmosphere of depravity and extravagance. However, the matter involves expenses, and it is difficult to avoid stagnation if simultaneous planning and care are not taken. Accordingly, please consult with your department to separately specify the number of sets of clothing that each student at each level of school should make each academic year, and the approximate amount of clothing fees that should be charged for strict implementation to show uniformity and ease of compliance. The student uniform regulations of this department were formulated and promulgated in April of the 18th year, and were notified in June of the same year that students at all levels of schools should uniformly wear uniforms from the 18th year. Now that the schools have not uniformly followed the regulations, they should be notified immediately to strive for uniformity. This is limited to the summer of this year. Except that primary schools can make appropriate changes in accordance with Article 9 of the student uniform regulations, other schools at all levels should strictly comply and must not delay. In addition, the student uniform regulations stipulate that uniforms are divided into winter and summer styles, and the materials must be completely domestic products. Schools at all levels must comply with this order, in addition to separate lines, and instruct all schools under their jurisdiction to comply with this order.

Ministry of Education instructs on educational matters in Shanghai 86

The Ministry of Education, according to the work report submitted by the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau from July to December of the 19th year, the Ministry of Education instructed that all the items in the report are fully understood. Regarding the various tasks of school education, such as running summer schools, stipulating the methods for primary school teachers to suspend repairs, and holding small-scale problems experiments, all are important. The methods and processes of the small-scale problems experiments should be reported at any time so that they can be published in the bulletin of this department as experimental research materials for various places. However, there are several matters that need attention: (1) There are too many out-of-school children in Shanghai. Every time there is an entrance examination, the schools are full. Primary schools should add or increase levels as much as possible to remedy this. (2) Teachers should be given generous rewards for further education. Those who have won awards should be given job security and qualification promotion. Active encouragement has a more effective effect. (3) The anti-corruption measures for school finances should be examined in detail and implemented conscientiously in light of the actual situation. The bureau may entrust accountants to check the accounts to supplement the shortcomings of the open financial methods and ensure that every penny is for public use. The style of integrity clears the accumulated ills and attaches importance to public funds from the school. (4) The selection of principals for primary and secondary schools should pay close attention to both qualifications and experience. Those who are filling the ranks should be eliminated. Those who have no practical experience should also be carefully examined to prevent those who are lucky enough to be admitted. (The following is omitted)

Establishment of Education Associations in Districts One, Two, and Three 87

Responsible person for District Nine to be elected today.

District One: The First District Education Association of Shanghai held its inaugural meeting at the Municipal Wu Ben Girls' Middle School at 2:00 PM yesterday. Over 300 members were present. After the formalities, Tao Baichuan, Huang Zaoxiong, Wu Bokang, the chairman of the preparatory committee, and Zhu Chengfu, the recorder, were publicly elected as temporary chairmen. (1) The chairman reported on the purpose of the meeting. (2) The members of the preparatory committee reported on the preparatory process, the work situation, the expenditure of funds, and the qualifications of members. Next, Comrade Mao from the Municipal Party Committee gave a speech, and Li Dachao from the Municipal Education Bureau delivered a speech. Next, the charter was discussed. Chairman Tao Baichuan read each article aloud, and after slight modifications, the entire charter was passed. Next, the directors were elected. The chairman appointed Zhang Yongchun, Zheng Tan, Li Bojun, and He Ziguo as tellers, Zhu Yakui and Zhou Yongnan as ballot collectors, and Zhou Puyin and Zhu Chunsheng as tally clerks. Zhao Luqing received 76 votes, and Li Bojun received 72 votes and were elected as alternate directors.

Afterwards, Zhabei's Goal Faced Many Threats. Goalkeeper Jiang Zongjin Showed Great Skill, Repeatedly Seizing the Ball from the Enemy's Iron Cavalry, Protecting the Goal. His Contribution Was Great. The Result Was a 1-1 Draw.

Local News

Naval Training Plane Crash Yesterday, Injuring People 102

Jiangluan Aircraft Crashed Southwest of Hongqiao Yesterday. Chen Changcheng and Lin Qingyun Tragically Lost Their Lives. The Remains Will Be Transported to Fujian by the Chu Tai Warship This Morning. Naval Aviation Officer Chen Changcheng and Trainee Lin Qingyun Were Aboard the Jiangluan Training Aircraft Yesterday at 10:00 AM at Hongqiao Airfield for Aviation Practice. While Practicing Small Turns About Five Miles Southwest of the Field, the Aircraft Suddenly Went Out of Control, Spinning and Plunging Downward Like a Shooting Arrow. With a Loud Crash, Both Men and the Aircraft Crashed into a Wheat Field in Qigu Shen Township. Training Officer Chen Changcheng Died Immediately, and Trainee Lin Qingyun Also Died of Severe Injuries Within Two Hours Despite Rescue Efforts. The Aircraft's Nose and Wings Were Smashed to Pieces, Leaving Only the Rear Half of the Fuselage. This Can Be Said to Be Another Unfortunate Incident in the Aviation World Recently.

Photograph of Training Officer Chen Changcheng's Remains

Details of the Aircraft Accident: The Naval Aviation Department Originally Had Four Training Officers: Chen Changcheng, He Jian, Jie Chengdong, and Peng Xi, as Well as One Western Training Officer and Fourteen Trainees Including Lin Qingyun. There Were a Total of Thirteen Training Aircraft, Six Manufactured by the Fuzhou Aircraft Factory and the Rest Purchased from Abroad, Including Five Masters Aircraft and Two Hengguo Aircraft. The Director of the Naval Aviation Department Is Concurrently the Director of the Shanghai Aircraft Factory, Shen Dexie. Therefore, Naval Officers Practiced Aviation at Hongqiao Airfield. Usually, Two Masters Aircraft Were Parked at Hongqiao Airfield. The Training Officers and Trainees Would Go There in Shifts Every Day from 7:00 AM to 12:00 PM for Flight Practice. The People of Shanghai Heard the Rattling of Aircraft Engines Every Morning and Saw the Silver-Gray Aircraft Soaring in the Clouds During These Practice Sessions. However, It Is Now Known That Yesterday Morning at 10:00 AM, Training Officer Chen and Trainee Lin Were Flying the Jiangluan Aircraft for Training When the Tragedy Suddenly Occurred. The Jiangluan Aircraft Was a 100-Horsepower Masters Aircraft with Two Seats in the Front and Rear. Yesterday Morning, Training Officer Chen Sat in the Front and Lin Sat in the Rear. According to Witnesses, Lin Was Practicing Small Turns About Five Miles Southwest of the Field, Only a Hundred Feet Above the Ground. The Aircraft Turned East for a Small Turn, But Suddenly Would Not Obey Orders, and Corrective Measures Were Not Effective. In a Hurry, It Turned into a Spiral and Plunged Straight Down. With a Loud Crash, The Aircraft's Nose Crashed into the Ground, and the Fuselage Flipped Forward. At That Time, Gao Qingshu and Other Naval Aviation Department Staff Members at the Airfield Saw the Aircraft Spinning Downward and Not Rising Again. Knowing Something Was Wrong, They Hurried to Investigate. Upon Reaching Qigu Shen Township, They Indeed Saw the Aircraft Accident. They Quickly Began Rescue Efforts, But Training Officer Chen, Sitting in the Front, Was Covered in Blood and Had Already Stopped Breathing. Lin Was Severely Injured and Unconscious, But Still Had a Faint Breath. The Crowd Carried Chen and Lin to the Airfield and Sent Chen's Body by Car to the International Funeral Home. Lin Was Sent by Car to the Fenglin Bridge Orthopedic Hospital for Treatment. Dr. Niu First Administered a Heart Stimulant for Emergency Treatment, But Lin's Injuries Were Too Severe to Save, and He Died Shortly After. His Body Was Also Sent by Car to the International Funeral Home. This Reporter Went to Hongqiao Airfield Yesterday After Hearing the News and Saw That Only the Remaining Fuselage of the Jiangluan Aircraft Was Left, Completely Destroyed and Beyond Repair. The Aircraft Was Purchased from the United Kingdom Last Year for Over 10,000 Gold Coins.

The Remains Will Be Shipped to Fujian This Morning. The Remains of Chen and Lin Were Sent One After Another by Naval Aviation Department Personnel to the International Funeral Home on Jiaozhou Road. Training Officers, Trainees, and Naval Aviation Department Personnel Went to Offer Condolences. The Coffins Were Placed There Yesterday Afternoon at 6:00 PM. The Details of the Accident Were Telegraphed to Naval Vice Minister Chen Shaokuan, Who Expressed Deep Grief Upon Hearing the News. He Specifically Instructed the Naval Department to Dispatch the Chu Tai Warship at 8:00 AM This Morning to Transport the Remains of Chen and Lin Back to Their Ancestral Home in Fuzhou. After Receiving the Order, The Chu Tai Warship Had Been Docked on the Huangpu River at Gaochang Temple, Building a Fire and Waiting to Depart. The Entire Naval Band Will Also Be There to Send Them Off. The Navy Will Also Lower the Flag to Half-Mast Today to Show Mourning.

Brief Biographies of Chen and Lin: Chen Changcheng, Originally Named Chen Changchen, Was from Fuzhou, 28 Years Old, and Unmarried. He Only Had One Older Sister in Shanghai. Chen Graduated from the Naval Flight and Submersible School With a Major in Aircraft Manufacturing. He Was Later Assigned to the Naval Aviation Department to Study Flight. He Graduated Last June With a Flight Record of Over 120 Hours. He Is Currently a Junior Flight Instructor at the Department, and He Worked Very Hard in Training Students. Lin Qingyun Was Also from Fuzhou, 20 Years Old. In 1929, He Received Aviation Knowledge at the Fuzhou Naval Aviation School. After One Year, He Was Assigned to the Naval Aviation Department to Study Flight. He Is Now Able to Fly Solo for Over 50 Hours. The Department's Rules State That He Can Graduate After Flying for 100 Hours.

"Dear Sir, My Lawyer Is Handling The Jin Li Yuan Wharf Arbitration Case. My Lawyer Negotiated Back And Forth With Father Xiaqi Of Santitude Hall. On The Thirteenth Of This Month, My Lawyer, On Behalf Of My Company, Held His Business Card And, Together With The French Municipal Council Member Mr. Zhang Jixian, Visited To Discuss The Sale Price. Fearing That My Lawyer Would Not Understand, He Repeated The Above In Shanghai Dialect, Openly Insulting Him, Which Was Beyond Reason. It Is Permissible Under The Laws Of All Countries To Bargain. Although The Father Represents The Church, I Am Afraid That Your Country Has No Church That Can Force Others To Obey The Selling Price. This Attitude Resembles The Ancient Roman Pope. My Lawyer Followed Your Consul General's Guiding Principle Of Settling Matters Peacefully, Endured It On The Spot And Did Not Clash Immediately, And Still Sent A Letter To Continue Negotiating In The Hope Of Settling The Case. Yesterday, Lawyer Baho Sent A Letter On Behalf Of The Church, Which Stated: 'We Now Have A Letter From Santitude Hall To Your Lawyer On The Seventeenth Of This Month To Father Xiaqi, The Manager Of The Church, Entrusting This Lawyer To Reply On His Behalf, As Follows: According To Your Letter, The China Merchants Bureau Is Willing To Purchase All Wharf And Shengke Ownership Of The Jin Li Yuan Wharf Registered Under A No. 69 For 200,000 Shanghai Universal Silver Dollars, Including In It. The Price Differs By As Much As 190,000 Silver Dollars From The 390,000 Taels Requested By My Client On November 3, 1930. My Client Believes That The Matter Is Difficult To Approach And There Is No Need To Continue Negotiations. Please Formally Inform The China Merchants Bureau That The Asking Price Of 390,000 Taels For Selling The Property Registered Under A No. 69 To The China Merchants Bureau On November 3, 1930, Has Now Been Unconditionally Withdrawn, Etc.' This Is A Fundamental Overturn. It Seems That The Father Has No Sincerity In Handling Matters, His Actions Are Almost Childish, And He Disregards The Diplomatic Relations Between China And France, Ignoring The Hard Work Of The Consul General And The Various Authorities In Mediating. The China Merchants Bureau Already Has Various Plans And Preparations For The Land Because The Other Party Allowed The Sale, And It May Not Be Convenient To Allow The Withdrawal Lightly. This Concerns A Breakdown In Mediation. I Am Sending You A Special Letter And Hope That You Will Strongly Maintain The Public Interest. Respectfully Submitted To The French Consul General In Shanghai, China Merchants Bureau Arbitrator Lawyer Gao Shuo."

Inspection of Foreign Passports to be Extended 110

Said to be Extended to May 1st. The matter of inspecting the passports of foreigners entering China has been decided by Chief Chen of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, who has decided to rent a building in Wusong to establish a foreign affairs sub-section and has transferred Chen Timing to be the deputy director of the foreign affairs section. Chen Timing will lead the inspectors to Wusong to start operations immediately. It was originally scheduled to be established on the 25th of this month, and starting from April 1st, all foreign ships entering the port would be inspected according to regulations. A request has been submitted to the Municipal Government and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to notify the embassies and consulates of various countries in China. It is now learned that the consulates of various countries in this port do not object to the Municipal Public Security Bureau's implementation of passport inspections for foreigners entering the country. However, it seems too hasty to implement the inspections starting from April 1st. The postal ships and world-class ships of various countries have already been opened before receiving the notification, and many passengers may not have prepared their passports. If the inspections are implemented for these ships, which are expected to arrive in Shanghai in mid-April, it will cause many obstacles. It would be best to implement the inspections at the beginning of May, so that all ships have received the notification, and foreigners coming to China will have completed their passport procedures. Chief Chen realized that the information provided by the consulates was accurate. To avoid conflicts, he decided to extend the implementation period. He instructed the inspectors to actively practice. It is now heard that Chief Chen intends to extend the establishment of the foreign affairs sub-section to April 15th and implement the inspections starting from May 1st.

Qin Runqing Talks About the Need for Qianzhuang Law 111

Qianzhuang are mainly based on credit lending, fundamentally different from banks. A reporter from New Voice News Agency specifically visited Qin Runqing, a standing committee member of the Qianye Gonghui, yesterday to inquire about his views on the Qianye Gonghui's request to the National Government for the enactment of a separate Qianzhuang Law. Qin's reply was quite important, and the main points are as follows: Although both the banking and qianzhuang industries are financial institutions, they are fundamentally different. Qianzhuang lending is based on the borrower's credit, which has always been the case. After the opening of trade, although Shanghai also imitated the foreign financial industry's practice of using collateral for lending, it was still a minority. As for the interior, the old morality of thousands of years and the old habits of hundreds of years are based on credit lending. For example, when tea is launched in the first half of the year and flowers and rice are launched in the second half of the year, the loans granted to merchants are all credit loans. Therefore, farmers and merchants have been accustomed to this practice for thousands of years, and it is indispensable. Secondly, small and medium-sized stores with capital of only 10,000 or 20,000 yuan, or several thousand yuan, often have a business volume that exceeds their capital by several times, which also relies on the credit loans of qianzhuang for assistance. Moreover, China does not have large merchants to support small and medium-sized merchants, so preventing the monopoly of large merchants is of direct benefit to farmers and workers, and is in line with Dr. Sun Yat-sen's policy of regulating capital and supporting farmers and workers. Therefore, restricting credit lending to qianzhuang will not only hinder qianzhuang but also have a great impact on society. The organization of qianzhuang is a partnership, and the shareholders bear unlimited liability. There are also very strict industry regulations to protect the credit of the industry. If qianzhuang are subordinate to the Banking Law, in addition to the stagnation of funds, the suspicion of investors, and the difficulty of reorganizing the company, there are other difficulties. The assets of the shareholders are mostly cash, which is deposited in A today and deposited in B tomorrow, or used for other businesses, and there is no certainty. If it is disclosed to the outside world, it will be shunned by the business community. Therefore, it is practically impossible to report the property certificate. As for the amount of capital, it should be determined according to the local commercial situation. If it is limited to a fixed number, it may not be possible to collect a large amount of funds in rural towns. When the country is currently unable to establish agricultural and industrial banks throughout the country, if the original qianzhuang are restricted by regulations and unable to maintain their current status, the funds of rural towns, farmers, and workers will inevitably not be able to be circulated. Other issues, such as business hours, are too rigid, and business procedures are more cumbersome, are minor issues. In short, national laws and regulations should be popularized in rural towns and remote areas, and should not only be applied to large cities.

Jinghu Train Delayed Yesterday 112

Locomotive derailed, trunk line blocked. At around 10:00 AM yesterday morning, a locomotive C49 derailed on a branch line for unloading mud at the Hepingmen Station on the Jinghu Railway while shunting cars to the main line. A body floated up in the river in Puzhong yesterday, hands tied with hemp rope to the neck, seemingly strangled and thrown into the river. The Nun Qing Shan's Eloquent Defense in the Case of Illegally Excavating the Coffin of the Seventh-Generation Ancestor 116

Converting Private Property to Repay the Monastery's Public Debt; Coffins of Fellow Monks, Not Ancestral Tombs. Gen Lin, the abbess of the Guanyin Hall on Lujia, Changbin Road, Public Concession, previously filed a lawsuit through her lawyer, Yan Lv, accusing her disciple, Qing Shan, of stealing and selling the tomb of her seventh-generation ancestral teacher and abandoning seven coffins. The case has been repeatedly investigated by the Shanghai Local Court Prosecutor's Office, but has been delayed until now without a verdict because Qing Shan has not yet appeared in court. The details have been reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that Qing Shan returned to Shanghai from Putuo yesterday. After learning that she had been accused by her teacher, Gen Lin, she hired a lawyer to file a counterclaim and voluntarily surrendered to the court, requesting that the court summon witnesses for cross-examination. The main points of the reasons presented by the nun Qing Shan are as follows:

Selling Land to Repay Debts The nun Qing Shan is currently forty-four years old and is from Zhejiang. In the second year of the Republic of China, she entered the monastery and became a disciple of Gen Lin. In the fourth year, she was promoted to be the manager of the monastery, and has been in charge for seventeen years. She has repaired many temples and Buddhist statues, accumulating debts totaling 2,000 gold. Until last year, due to the pressure of creditors, she had no choice but to sell her private property cemetery (two acres and six fen of cemetery land in the 28th district and 6th ward of the Fahua District) to pay off the debts.

The Tomb is Private The monastery submitted a request to the National Government for temple registration on May 20, 1929. At that time, the manager of the monastery, Nun Qing Shan, submitted her name and attached a photo of Qing Shan. The cemetery in the Fahua District is private property and has not been registered. Therefore, the nun believes that she has the right to sell the land and use the proceeds to repay the debts owed by the monastery for repairing temples and Buddhist statues over the years. All evidence will be presented in court during the trial.

Relocation to Public Cemetery Regarding the alleged excavation of the tombs of the seventh-generation ancestral teacher, the tombs are not the tombs of the ancestral teacher. The seven coffins buried in the tombs are all of fellow monks. They have now been relocated to the Yongnian Public Cemetery. The cost of cremation and burial is 100 taels of silver per coffin, plus transportation costs, totaling 800 taels of silver. It can be said that the remains have been abandoned.

Rong Xiang Becomes an Enemy There are five nuns in the monastery, including Rong Xiang, who is young and does not abide by the monastic rules, resulting in her being pregnant. She went to Hangzhou in June last year to give birth to a daughter. At that time, Qing Shan advised her not to listen, but instead became an enemy, resulting in this lawsuit. Qing Shan has now presented two letters from her master (describing the situation in the hospital) sent by the nun Rong Xiang last year from the Guanyin Nunnery on Jie Dai Temple Port, Hushu, Hangzhou, as strong evidence.

Preparing to File a Counterclaim Qing Shan has now collected evidence of the privately owned cemetery in the Fahua District and is preparing to summon witnesses for cross-examination in court to find out the truth. All counterclaim sections are now being drafted by a lawyer for submission.

Continued Trial of Bandits for Kidnapping and Extortion 117

In addition to the kidnapping of Li Huiqing, there are also three cases of extortion. On February 8th of this year, at 1:40 AM, Hui Yunfang, the Ningbo manager of the Xielong Real Estate Company, a Sino-Japanese joint venture located at 313 Yingchunfang, Hubei Road, was about to be kidnapped by bandits, but they mistakenly kidnapped Hui's friend, Li Huiqing. Li was later released for a ransom of 2,000 yuan. However, after this incident, Hui repeatedly received threatening letters from the bandits, attempting to extort tens of thousands of silver dollars. Hui's representative, Zeng Yisheng, reported the case to the Lao Zha Public Concession Police. Chinese Detective You Agen, detectives Song Bingzheng, Liu Junqing, Liu Chunshu, and others arrested Zhou Linsheng from Pudong, Lu Agen from Yangzhou, and Zhou's mistress, Xu Yuying, and Lu's mistress, Wang Genmei, at the Huizhong Hotel and other places. They were handed over to the Special District Local Court for questioning and investigation. Yesterday afternoon, Criminal Tribunal Chief Xu Jiashi opened the court to continue the trial. The female defendant Wang Genmei was not brought to court because she was in labor. According to the police lawyer, the defendants are accused of kidnapping Li Huiqing, and Zhou Linsheng and Lu Agen are also accused of writing threatening letters in three cases. The defendants are ordered to present their case first.

The Circumstances of the Kidnapping of Li Huiqing Li's friend Hui Yunfang has a car with license plate number 8743. Hui goes to a certain room in the East Asia Hotel every night for entertainment. On the night of the kidnapping, Hui happened to have something to do and was not in his car, so he lent it to Li Huiqing. Li, along with his friend Chou Bingrong and Chou's son Chou Bingheng, rode in the car. When they drove to Nanjing Road near Guangxi Road, several bandits suddenly rushed out and asked if Hui Yunfang was in the car. Li and others replied that Hui was not in the car. The bandits then questioned each person's name and recognized that Li Huiqing was qualified to be kidnapped. They drove Chou and his son off the car, and Chou Bingrong's leather coat was also stripped off. Then, they took Li to Lu Agen's house on the overpass at 15 Ershi East Road, French Concession, and locked Li's hands and feet with iron chains. Later, Li's wife contacted the bandits. The bandits sent Xu Yuying as a representative to negotiate. As a result, Li was released for a ransom of 2,000 yuan. After Li escaped, he went to the police station to report the incident. Therefore, the defendants Lu Agen and Xu Yuying are actually the main offenders. However, when Wang Genmei was arrested, a pawn ticket was found on her person. The detective traced the pawn ticket to Wanjic Pawnshop on Aivenyi Road and retrieved the leather coat stripped from Chou Bingrong. The detective took it to Chou's house for him to identify whether it was the original stolen item. Chou suddenly denied that the leather coat had been stripped off. However, he did report to the police station at the time that a leather coat had been robbed. The plaintiff and witnesses in the kidnapping case have not arrived in court today. The court should issue a warrant to summon them. Since the last adjournment, the police have ordered detectives to arrest the gang leader Fang at 179 Nancheng Dulu. However, he had already fled upon hearing the news. Only two pieces of paper were seized, which recorded the distribution of the loot. Lu Agen and others each received one share, while Xu Yuying received one and a half shares. According to the police investigation, the funds used before the kidnapping were all advanced by Xu Yuying, so she received half a share more than others. An iron chain and two pairs of sunglasses were also seized from Lu Agen's house at 15 Ganshijie Road, French Concession. However, the defendant Zhou Linsheng was not at the scene when the kidnapping took place, and only committed the crime of writing threatening letters. Therefore, the police did not prosecute Zhou for the kidnapping case. As for the charges of extortion and fraud committed by these people, there are (1) a threatening letter written to Yuanfengshun Candle Shop at 893 Zhejiang Road on January 1st of this year, attempting to defraud several thousand silver dollars, (2) a similar method used to threaten Mo Jingshan, the owner of Taifeng Pawnshop at 514 Kaifeng Road, on February 2nd of this year, attempting to extort a large sum of money because they failed to kidnap Mo, and then wrote threatening letters, and (3) an extortion case against Sanyang South Goods Store at 528 Nanjing Road in 1918. All witnesses have been summoned to court for questioning. Then, the threatening letters were presented to the court as evidence. According to the complaint of Zeng Yisheng, the representative of the plaintiff Hui Yunfang, Hui has gone to Ningbo and cannot be present today. Questioned the defendant Lu Agen, who confessed that the remaining room was rented by Fang, and that he did not know about the kidnapping. The defendant Xu Yuying confessed that she was contacted by the fugitive Fang and Agen to contact Li Huiqing, but she did not know what it was about. Later, she went to Li's house in Zhilanfang, Baxianqiao, and obtained 2,000 silver dollars. Fang gave me 150 yuan, but I actually received 40 yuan, and the remaining silver was borrowed by Fang. Zhou Linsheng has been having an affair with her since last year, etc. The victims who received the threatening letters testified to the court about the circumstances of the case. Lu Agen hired lawyer E Sen to defend him. Judge Xu verified the confession and ordered the defendants to be detained separately pending a rescheduled trial, as the case still needs to be investigated.

New Building of the Young Women's Christian Association to be Completed Soon 119

Meeting Scheduled to Discuss Association Affairs. The national association of the Young Women's Christian Association of China has been building a new association building on Yuanmingyuan Road. The seven-story building has been completed, and it is expected that all of the eighth-story main building and the rooftop attic will be completed by Easter. The association is located behind the British Consulate, and the view of the Huangpu River can be seen from the second floor and above, which is an excellent location. The land was purchased in 1919 by the National Young Women's Christian Association of America and transferred to the National Association of the Young Women's Christian Association of China for safekeeping in 1927. Initially, there were three old houses. It was decided to rebuild the building at the annual meeting in 1929, and Madam Mei Huaquan was appointed as the chairman of the construction committee. The plan was drawn and donations were raised. So far, 70% of the construction funds have been raised. The remaining funds will be borrowed from various banks. After completion, it is planned to lease the floors below the seventh floor and use the interest to repay the loan. The eighth floor will be reserved for the association's offices and meeting places. The association is scheduled to hold a joint meeting of all committee members and directors in the new association building on the sixth floor this Wednesday to report on the progress of the new association building and discuss the association's affairs.

Horse Riding School Offers Special Treatment to Chinese 120

The Yiding Pan Da West Horse Riding School has been established for more than ten years. Its facilities are complete, and it has a total of more than 200 horses. Dozens of people go to learn riding skills every day, and hundreds of people have graduated. All of them are well-known figures in the Chinese and Western business and political circles. According to the school's regulations, one course consists of 35 lessons and is completed in five weeks. The teaching method is different every week, so after completing one course, students can become proficient in various riding techniques. It is said that in recent years, more Westerners have learned to ride horses. Chinese people often feel that the fees are too high, or think that horse riding is prone to danger, or think that there are no suitable places. In fact, the horses in ordinary stables have not been trained and are wild and difficult to tame, which can easily lead to falls. The horses in this school have been trained for a long time and can be commanded freely, so there is absolutely no other danger. In terms of expenses, in order to give special treatment to Chinese people, special group study classes are now offered, and the tuition fees are specially reduced, so that our young students have the opportunity to learn to ride horses. School students are especially welcome. They can learn from 6:00 AM to 8:00 PM. The methods are: (1) For groups or students with more than 10 people, the tuition fee will be reduced by one-half of the original price. For more than 100 people, only one-fifth will be charged. Both men and women are welcome, and each school is specially allowed one free teacher. (2) For places that are too far away, such as Jiangwan and Yangshupu, the school can send coaches to lead the horses to nearby open spaces for training. Riding skills are the best method of whole-body exercise and are not limited to men, women, old, and young. Recently, the school entrusted Xie Hong of Shenbao to contact people from all walks of life.

Fined 100 Yuan. Shipwrecked Teen Attempts Suicide 122

Luckily Encountered Mr. Du Who Provided Assistance. Yesterday morning at 0:45 AM, a young man hired sampan number 1067 at the Jiujiang Road wharf, claiming he would pay two dimes to cross to Pudong. Unexpectedly, when the boat reached the center of the river, the young man suddenly jumped into the water, intending to commit suicide. Although it was dark, the boatman quickly rescued him before he drowned completely. He was then sent to the water police station. According to his statement, his name is Wu Yutian, also known as Bao Lin, 19 years old, from Shengze County, Jiangsu Province. He used to work at the sales department of the 別發 bookstore on Nanjing Road in the Public Concession. Later, he had disagreements with his colleagues and left his job in anger. His parents in his hometown had also passed away one after another. Coupled with being unemployed for a long time and being lonely, he felt that the circumstances were so dire, unlike anything he had encountered since birth. Therefore, he became tired of the world and wanted to commit suicide, and so on. The young man was good at English and conversed fluently with the Western officers in the police station. The head of the police ordered Chinese detective Ge Changsheng to send him to the residence of Mr. Du Yuesheng, a prominent figure in the French Concession, to find ways to help him. Mr. Du, considering Wu's situation to be truly pitiful, not only provided financial assistance on the spot but also introduced him to a job at the Race Club, so that he could live in peace, it is said.

Mrs. John Wah Dies. The Young Women's Christian Association received news from other sources a month ago that Mrs. John Wah had passed away in New York. She was respected by Chinese and foreign friends alike. Ms. Jingxia worked at the Chinese Young Women's Christian Association for a total of eighteen years. In 1928, the mother and daughter returned to their country for vacation. Mrs. Wah eventually succumbed to physical decline and was unable to revisit China. Last November, Mrs. Wah fell ill in New York and was treated by doctors, who announced her recovery. Unexpectedly, she passed away on February 16th. Her friends in China were deeply saddened upon hearing the news, it is said.

Flexible Measures for Cotton Fabric Unified Tax Waybill 129

The Unified Tax Department is dispatching personnel to be stationed permanently at the Cotton Fabric Association to handle matters. The Shanghai Cotton Fabric Association previously found the procedures for unified tax waybills to be inconvenient in various ways and dispatched representatives to the Ministry of Finance's Unified Tax Department to petition for changes and brought a formal presentation requesting approval. It is now reported that the Fifth Section of the Unified Tax Department sent a letter to the association yesterday, saying: "Regarding the various points presented in your letter of March 17th, we have informed the Director and discussed it with Director Wang. Regarding the matter of imitating the Customs Pass system, it is necessary to stipulate methods and printing, which may not be possible to handle in a short time. However, following the precedent of the Silk and Mercerized Cotton Weaving Industry Association, the Suzhou Bureau may assign personnel to be stationed at the association to handle the procedures for exchanging waybills. It seems that this can be implemented immediately. However, the Suzhou-Zhejiang-Anhui District Bureau wants to know the details. It is hoped that your association will nominate representatives to meet with Section Chief Chen of the Third Section of the Suzhou Bureau to obtain inquiries. As for the column for writing the destination of the tax certificate, it can be handled flexibly. Those who sell on the spot can fill in 'This Port.' Those who transport to various provinces can only fill in the two characters 'Other Ports' and pass through without obstruction." After receiving the letter, the Cotton Fabric Association immediately nominated four representatives, Chen, Li, Shi, and Ye, to meet with Section Chief Chen of the Third Section of the Suzhou Bureau. Section Chief Chen stated that the unified tax forms could be divided into several types in the future, such as one piece per sheet, five pieces per sheet, ten pieces per sheet, and so on, so that merchants could freely collect them according to their needs, which could save a lot of distribution procedures. However, because printing takes time, the bureau will first send two staff members to reside in the Cotton Fabric Association to handle distribution matters.

Labor-Management Negotiations in the Sanxin Yarn Factory Storm 130

Representatives from Both Sides Have Been Appointed. Employees Hold a Meeting to Divide Responsibilities. The Sanxin Yarn Factory on Yangshupu Road announced its sale, and the employees demanded a settlement of the aftermath, so the transfer has not yet been completed. The situation obtained yesterday is recorded as follows:

Yesterday's Situation. After the labor-management negotiations failed the night before, the Yangshupu Police Department increased the number of armed police stationed at the factory for protection. Yesterday morning, many workers still came to the factory to inquire about the resumption of work. In order to maintain order, the police still sent detectives to patrol inside and outside the factory. By 4:00 PM, the male and female workers waiting outside the factory had retreated slightly, so some of the armed detectives also withdrew, leaving only a few stationed inside the factory.

Negotiations Underway. The employee relief group returned to the factory to convene a meeting after the negotiations failed last night due to a dispute over the number of representatives. In order to respect the opinions of the factory owner, they made concessions and reduced the number of representatives to four. They also sent a letter to the factory owner at 11:00 PM, ordering someone to send it to Sheng Ze cheng's residence on Jing'an Temple Road. Unexpectedly, the doorman refused to accept the letter on the grounds that the young master was already asleep. The original letter to the factory owner is recorded below: "Respectfully, yesterday, Dongweng (respected sir) instructed all the employees in the factory to elect representatives to negotiate with Dongweng at the company today (referring to yesterday, the 20th). All the employees in the factory elected six staff members and three foreman to await your arrival for a joint meeting. However, Dongweng suddenly insisted that the number of representatives should be limited to four. In order to express their sincerity in harmonious consultation, the colleagues immediately returned to the factory and appointed He [name], etc., as representatives because Dongweng had already left the company today and there was no opportunity to meet in person. They specially sent a letter to Dador to allow them to listen to the instructions tomorrow. Please indicate when it will be. This is respectfully requested for the inspection of Ze Gong, Ping Gong, and Sheng Gong Dongweng. Employee representatives Sun He [name], Chen Youqing, worker representatives Yang Yuheng, Hou Jiahai, jointly on March 20." It is heard that the factory owner and Rong Zongjing have appointed Zhu Cheng as their fully empowered representative, but he has not yet come to contact them.

Employees Express Their Views. According to employees, Sanxin has been in operation for forty years since its opening, and it has been profitable every year, with total profits reaching tens of millions. This sudden sale was unexpected. Therefore, the terms of dissolution proposed by the colleagues are not excessive. (1) A factory that has been profitable for many years should not be compared with other factories that are operating at a loss when it is sold. (2) What Rong [name] bought was only 70,000 spindles and 1,000 looms, while the most important real estate still fell into the hands of foreigners. At a time when our country's industry is declining, such a large industry should not be split apart. If Rong [name] can completely buy it, then the colleagues may not be able to make concessions. The small matter of dissolution fees is small, but the loss of our country's sovereignty is great. The order in the factory is quite good.

Employee Congress. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, the Employee Relief Group convened a congress. More than a hundred people, including all staff members and worker representatives, attended. Chen Youqing was publicly elected as chairman. It was resolved to (1) establish seven sections: General Affairs, Documentation, Accounting, Public Relations, General Services, Communications, and Discipline, in order to protect the safety of the factory and facilitate negotiations; (2) The General Affairs Section will have one section chief and seven section members, and the company may participate with one person. The Documentation Section will have one section chief and five section members. The Accounting Section will have one section chief and two section members. The Public Relations Section will have one section chief and four section members. The General Services Section will have one section chief and ten section members. The Communications Section will have one section chief and four section members. The Discipline Section will have twenty staff members and twenty workers, divided into groups to take turns on duty to protect the machinery in the factory and maintain order; (3) Elect five councilors to deliberate on all negotiation matters.

Record of Meeting of the Industrial and Commercial Management Association 131

Wu Qingtai Speaks on His Impressions of Inspecting Industries in Europe. The Chinese Industrial and Commercial Management Association held a meeting yesterday afternoon at the Lianhua General Association on Beijing Road to invite Mr. Wu Qingtai, manager of the Shanghai Cement Company, to speak on his impressions of inspecting industries in Europe. Liu Hongsheng, Fu Bingwen, Shou Jingwei, Wu Yunshu, Chen Kuilai, and dozens of others, chaired by honorary director Cao Yunxiang, gathered for dinner. At the end of the dinner, the chairman stood up to deliver an introductory speech and report on the association's affairs as follows: (1) The association's advisors have been appointed and are ready to provide consultation to all parties and contribute to scientific management. (2) The Mechanical National Goods Factory Federation and the Commercial Press have organized a lecture series on scientific management issues, which has achieved excellent results and can be cooperated with by the association in the future. (3) At the second narrative meal of the association, it was resolved to organize a committee for the implementation of factory law. The chairman has appointed Li Zufan, Pan Gongzhan, Hu Shuhua, Ji Jiannan, and himself as committee members. The first committee meeting has been held and a presentation has been drafted to be printed and distributed to the national chambers of commerce for careful study before being submitted to the Legislative Yuan for revision and implementation of the difficulties. Next, Mr. Wu stood up to give a speech, and the main points are excerpted below: Qingtai was ordered by Liu Hongsheng, general manager of the factory, last September, and also entrusted by the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, to attend the 14th International Labor Conference held in Geneva by the representative of the capital side. During his time abroad in September, he did not dare to say that he had obtained all the secrets, but he gained many impressions. The following are the impressions gained from the Labor Conference: The International Labor Conference originated from the League of Nations. All countries attach great importance to it. Although the resolutions passed must be implemented after being approved by their respective governments, whenever representatives from various countries meet, they argue endlessly. The reason for this is to stop the so-called labor policy of the Soviet government, and the representatives sent by various countries are all first-class figures. For example, the British representative is Ms. Bonfield, the Minister of Labor, and her accompanying staff, advisors, and experts all have Japanese representatives with lavish demeanor. Since the establishment of the National Government of China, it has participated twice, including this time. The seat of this qualification problem has been the most important, although no one has raised questions, but can only be used to fill the number. The cases discussed during the meeting were all European countries issues. The representatives of the Eastern Japanese countries, although occasionally speaking, were all beautiful words, of little importance. He attended the meeting for seventeen days, without interruption. This can be said to be innocent to the people. He will not elaborate on the details. Regarding the management problem, he went to various countries in Europe and the United States to investigate after the meeting closed. He now has the following impressions: All countries are now very simple in management methods, because all parties have realized it, so the effect on management is very macro. There are three points in our country's workers that make scientific management very difficult: (1) People's habits are too deep (2) People's education is not very average (3) People's perseverance is not enough So there are these three points China's industry is not developed and the management is not proper, which reduces productivity. I hope that you will find ways to deal with the above three points as soon as possible. After the speech, there was thunderous applause, and the meeting was dismissed at half past two.

Family Inquiries. Yesterday morning at 7:00 AM, the families of the Changjiang Steamer's crew members in Shanghai saw the reports in the newspapers about the ship's accident and the arrival of the victims in Shanghai. They rushed to the Songshan Road Police Station to inquire, supporting the old and carrying the young. Xu Arui's elderly mother from Zhoushan, Zhejiang, who was over fifty years old, heard that her son had drowned in the ocean and burst into tears, so painful that she wanted to die. Her tragic situation made onlookers feel sad. After being persuaded by others, she began to cry and return. The rest who saw their family members returning alive were overjoyed and rushed to buy food and clothing to send to them.

Request for Relief. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, the shipwrecked crew members elected chief comprador Lin Fengshi as their representative to go to the Shanghai Steamer Company at 35 Renji Road to request relief. Manager Kang Zhenkui met with them and agreed to give each person a loss fee of 15 yuan. Lin thought the amount was too small and refused to accept it. He returned to report to the crew members. Second comprador Ling Hong, third comprador Lin Xiong, Huang Yaonan, Guo Yawu, Luo Jie, and Lu Shen six people reported the details of the accident to the Seamen's General Union and requested assistance.

Names of the Deceased. Seamen's General Union Negotiates Relief for Distressed Workers 135

The Seamen's General Union sent a letter to various shipping companies, saying: "It is reported by our secretary, Liu Yuzhou, that we have read in the newspapers that the China Merchants Bureau's Xinchang ship hit a reef and sank, drowning a western boy. The Shun Changhang Norwegian ship hit a reef and sank, and although the seamen escaped, their belongings were all flooded. The Shun Henghang Cookla ship caught fire while carrying explosives and sank, killing many seamen. The Dada Company's Daji ship sank due to negligence, killing more than a hundred people. The seamen were among them. We are deeply saddened by these tragic incidents and propose the following measures: (1) Order the Shanghai branch to investigate the names, addresses, and numbers of all injured and deceased seamen and notify their families to report the details of the accident to the union; (2) Send letters to the relevant companies of each ship to provide relief to the distressed workers and their families, and in the future, carefully select ship owners and Jiang captains and do not carry explosive materials; (3) Submit a presentation to the competent authorities of the union to forward instructions to the shipping companies to implement the second measure. For foreign companies, notify their consuls in China to inform them. This is a matter of providing relief to distressed workers and preventing future disasters, and it should be implemented urgently."

Petition for Aid from the Ba County Relief Committee 137

The Provisional Relief Committee of Ba County, Sichuan, wired as follows (abridged titles): "This year, misfortune continues to befall Sichuan. Last year, the rain was unseasonable, leading to spring floods and summer droughts. The harvest was poor, granaries are empty, the wealthy have become impoverished, and the poor are starving. Everywhere you look, the land is full of suffering. The news has spread far and wide, causing deep dismay. The vitality of the people has not yet recovered. Last winter, for a hundred days, there was no rain, and water sources dried up, causing the land to crack and split. The disaster is most severe in eastern Sichuan, which has always produced little rice and has a denser population than other areas. Ba County relies entirely on the assistance of the counties in upper Sichuan for its food supply. However, in this year of famine, everyone is struggling to take care of themselves, making it difficult to provide assistance. As a result, in recent months, there have been frequent prohibitions, cutting off supplies and causing rice prices to skyrocket. A single斗 of rice costs a hundred or a thousand, and there is not even any available to buy. Starving people cry out for food. The masses are wandering, creating unprecedented suffering. The people are the foundation of the nation, and food is the lifeblood of the people. The new harvest is still far off, and the vitality of the entire region is dwindling. If we reach the point where the old harvest is exhausted and the new harvest has not yet arrived, the suffering will be even greater. Thinking of the future, we cannot help but be alarmed. Therefore, on the 真 day of March, we gathered representatives from various agencies, France, and all sectors of society to establish the Provisional Relief Committee of Ba County in the county government. We also resolved to establish branch committees and offices in various districts, townships, and towns to urgently raise relief funds. However, the disaster is extremely severe and has reached a critical point. We hope that people from all walks of life will have compassion and empathy, and generously donate money and grain. Then, the hundreds of thousands of disaster victims in Ba County will be eternally grateful. We are sending this urgent telegram with utmost sincerity and await your command." The Ba County Provisional Relief Committee: Chairman Feng Junyi, Director of the General Affairs Section Xie Zhaolin, Committee Members Wu Xiangchi, Liu Zhusan, Shi Mingyuan, Zeng Ji, Liu Boyang, Deng Shouyi, Director of the Document Section Liu Gongzhu, Committee Members Long Teng, Yan Hengqiu, Huang Bozheng, Yang Chonghai, Director of the Finance Section Li Xinwu, Committee Members Li Renjing, Wang Lanji, Director of the Fundraising Section Wen Shaohe, Committee Members Li Kuian, Zhu Shuchi, Chen Zhuozhang, Zhao Zisheng, Hu Gancheng, Shi Rongting, 璯 Xiaoxian, He Fuzhou, respectfully.

Inspection Report of the Central Bank 138

The eighty-fourth report on the inspection of the issuance reserve of the Central Bank states: "In accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Ordinance, this committee is responsible for inspecting the reserve for the issuance of convertible banknotes of the Central Bank. The eighty-fourth inspection was held at the Issuance Bureau of the Central Bank on March 20, 1931. The results of the inspection are announced as follows: Total amount of convertible banknotes issued: 28,766,952 silver dollars, including 27,900,802 silver dollar banknotes and 860,150 auxiliary currency banknotes. Total amount of convertible banknote reserve: 28,766,952 silver dollars, including 21,585,912 silver dollars in cash reserve, of which 14,358,232.25 silver dollars are stored in the Issuance Bureau of the Central Bank, 2,009,707 silver dollars are stored in branches in various ports, and 5,217,972.75 silver dollars are deposited with other banks. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 7,181,040 silver dollars. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank Convertible Banknote Regulations, the cash reserve should be 60% and the guarantee reserve should be 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is less than 40%, which is in compliance with the regulations. This report is hereby issued." March 20, 1931, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank: Li Fuxun, Supervisors: Wang Jingli, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jilun.

Navy Department to Recruit Students This Year 140

The Navy Department has been striving for development in recent years. In addition to adding warships and ordering cruisers from a certain country for 12 million yuan of national currency, it is also planning to promote naval education. This year, the Fuzhou (Mawei) Naval Academy has been approved by the Ministry to recruit 100 students for the navigation and mechanical engineering departments. All students of Chinese nationality who are at least 14 years old, approximately 5 feet tall, weigh 85 pounds, have a dignified appearance, clear features, are not nearsighted, have no hidden illnesses, can write essays in Chinese, can construct short sentences in English, and have studied common fractions and decimals in arithmetic may be recommended by their respective provincial governments. The recommended students must bring the recommendation letter, along with two 4-inch half-length photos of themselves with their name, place of origin, age, and three generations noted on the back, to the Navy Department in the capital for a physical examination by June 1st. The departmental examinations will be held on the 16th. Those recommended by naval officers of the rank of lieutenant commander or above must submit the recommendation letter, along with two 4-inch half-length photos of the student with the same information noted on the back, to the Navy Department by May 1st.

Xia Jiujin, a Child with Six Fingers, Goes Missing 141

Abducted by bandits, Xia Jiujin, a twelve-year-old boy from Shaoxing, the son of a Xia family in the Dasheng Warehouse at the Xintai Wharf in Nanshi, disappeared yesterday after playing outside the door. His parents are both old and have only this one child, so they are urgently searching everywhere, but there is no trace of him. They are extremely distraught and have repeatedly tried to commit suicide, but were fortunately discovered and persuaded to stop. They immediately reported the incident to the Municipal Public Security Bureau and various district offices, requesting them to pay attention. The appearance and clothing are as follows: fair complexion, six fingers on the right hand, wearing black twill cotton trousers, a black cloth long gown, and green "Equality" shoes.
